You are a strict failure-mode judge for visual geometry benchmark tasks. Use only the provided task card and evidence. Return valid JSON that matches the requested schema.

Classify each attempt below into exactly one failure mode.

Allowed labels:
- Evasion / Forfeit
- Trivialized / Misframed
- Runaway Overthinking
- Local-Only (Global Constraint Integration Failure)
- Near-Miss Edge Case

Rules:
- You must output one decision per listed subpass.
- Listed subpasses: 7, 8, 12
- Base justification on verifier signals and model output/COT evidence.
- Do not invent constraints absent from the task card.
- Runaway Overthinking requires BOTH (a) COT evidence of spiraling or overcomplicated reasoning AND (b) diverse error types in the verifier signal. Repeated instances of the same error type indicate a systematic Local-Only failure, not Runaway.

Task Card:
# Task q54: VGB4 - Half Subdivision Neighbours
- Source file: `54.py`
- Taxonomy: `FAILURE_TAXONOMY.md`
- Run cards dir: `experiments/failure_mode_analysis/failure_mode_task_cards/cards/gpt-5.2-chat-azure-Reasoning/`

## Intent
Test exact discrete neighbor inference in recursively subdivided spaces using bitstring leaf identifiers.

## Output Contract
- Prompted format is a comma-separated list of leaf labels (quotes optional); the prompt may also request a leading `<thinking>...</thinking>` block (which the parser strips).
- The grader accepts either a raw list / comma-separated sequence *or* an object with `neighbors`.
- Neighbor labels are bitstring leaf identifiers (strings of `0/1`, with `""` allowed for the root in some cases).

## Hard Constraints (Verifier-Checked)
- Neighbor label schema.
- Exact expected neighbor set match.
- Order-independent comparison; duplicates are invalid.
- Handles varied axis-ordering/task variants through curated dataset.

## Verifier Signals
| Signal/Error | Meaning | Likely failure mode(s) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `missing: [...]` | Required neighbors omitted | `Local-Only`, `Near-Miss` |
| `extra: [...]` | Non-neighbors included | `Local-Only`, `Near-Miss` |
| `errors: [...]` | Invalid label format/structure | `Trivialized`, `Evasion` |

## Failure-Mode Tie-Breaks (Task-Specific)
- `Evasion / Forfeit`: Missing `neighbors` payload.
- `Trivialized / Misframed`: Non-bitstring or unrelated output form.
- `Runaway Overthinking`: COT shows spiraling tree-traversal reasoning that produces diverse error types (malformed identifiers AND wrong count AND format failures).
- `Local-Only (Global Constraint Integration Failure)`: Broad neighbor-set mismatch.
- `Near-Miss Edge Case`: Single neighbor missing/extra.

## Judge Input Bundle
1. Prompt (subdivision tree + target leaf).
2. Raw output.
3. Parsed `neighbors`.
4. Verifier diff.
5. Optional reasoning summary.

## Classification Prompt Snippet
```text
Classify q54 with one failure mode.
Prioritize schema validity and neighbor-set diff size.
Return JSON: failure_mode, confidence, justification.
```

def get_bounding_box(path):
    """Compute the bounding box for a node given its path."""
    x_range = [0.0, 1.0]
    y_range = [0.0, 1.0]
    z_range = [0.0, 1.0]
    
    for level, bit in enumerate(path):
        axis = get_axis_at_level(level)
        
        if axis == 'x':
            mid = (x_range[0] + x_range[1]) / 2
            if bit == '0':
                x_range[1] = mid
            else:
                x_range[0] = mid
        elif axis == 'y':
            mid = (y_range[0] + y_range[1]) / 2
            if bit == '0':
                y_range[1] = mid
            else:
                y_range[0] = mid
        elif axis == 'z':
            mid = (z_range[0] + z_range[1]) / 2
            if bit == '0':
                z_range[1] = mid
            else:
                z_range[0] = mid
    
    return (x_range, y_range, z_range)

```python
def ranges_overlap(r1, r2):
    """Check if two 1D ranges overlap."""
    return r1[0] < r2[1] and r2[0] < r1[1]

def ranges_overlap_2d(r1_a, r1_b, r2_a, r2_b):
    """Check if two 2D rectangular regions overlap."""
    return ranges_overlap(r1_a, r2_a) and ranges_overlap(r1_b, r2_b)

def boxes_share_face(box1, box2):
    """Check if two boxes share a face."""
    (x1, y1, z1) = box1
    (x2, y2, z2) = box2
    
    eps = 1e-10  # Small epsilon for floating point comparison
    
    # Check x-adjacent (share a yz-face)
    if (abs(x1[1] - x2[0]) < eps or abs(x1[0] - x2[1]) < eps):
        if ranges_overlap_2d(y1, z1, y2, z2):
            return True
    
    # Similar checks for y-adjacent and z-adjacent faces
    if (abs(y1[1] - y2[0]) < eps or abs(y1[0] - y2[1]) < eps):
        if ranges_overlap_2d(x1, z1, x2, z2):
            return True
    
    if (abs(z1[1] - z2[0]) < eps or abs(z1[0] - z2[1]) < eps):
        if ranges_overlap_2d(x1, y1, x2, y2):
            return True
    
    return False
```

    return (x_min, x_max, y_min, y_max)

def shares_edge(bbox1, bbox2):
    """Check if two bounding boxes share an edge (not just a corner)"""
    x1_min, x1_max, y1_min, y1_max = bbox1
    x2_min, x2_max, y2_min, y2_max = bbox2
    
    # Check if they share a vertical edge
    if x1_max == x2_min or x1_min == x2_max:
        # Check if y ranges overlap (not just touch at a point)
        y_overlap_min = max(y1_min, y2_min)
        y_overlap_max = min(y1_max, y2_max)
        if y_overlap_max > y_overlap_min:
            return True
    
    # Check if they share a horizontal edge
    if y1_max == y2_min or y1_min == y2_max:
        x_overlap_min = max(x1_min, x2_min)
        x_overlap_max = min(x1_max, x2_max)
        if x_overlap_max > x_overlap_min:
            return True
    
    return False
